AAA TV (SAT) 05/02/2026 Auditorio General José María Arteaga, Querétaro, Querétaro [AAA, LR Lucha LIbre]
1) Lince Dorado b Cruz del Toro, Octagón Jr.
## Start of pre-live matches. Lince beat Cruz.
2) La Parka, Mr. Iguana b Colmillo de Plata, Garra de Oro and Nobu San, Takuma and Forastero, Sansón
## Parka beat Sanson. After Parka & Iguana left, the War Raider walked out and destroyed the other three teams (including Kento, seconding his pals.)
3) Catalina b Jessy Jackson
## Surprisingly not a squash. Las Toxicas attacked Catalina after the match. Lola Vice first tried to make the save and finally Bayley - to a big reaction - cleaned house. Trios match teased.
4) Mini Vikingo b Hijo Del Vikingo
## Mini Vikingo won cleanly, though only after both got visual pins and Wagner 3 (announced to defend the AAA LA title against Hijo del Vikingo on 05/30) stopped the older Vikingo from using a chair. Omos attacked both Mini Vikingo and Wagner with Galeno del Mal returning to make the save.
5) Rey Fénix b Laredo Kid
## Fenix won clean with the Mexican muscle buster. Fenix offered a handshake post match but Laredo clutched his belt and brushed him off.
6) Galeno del Mal b Drago, Chris Carter
## Aired after live portion. Could've been a handicap match; Drago (still the Dragon Suicida third Drago) and Chris Carter never fought, never had a chance to fight in a short squash match where Galeno pinned both. Galeno del Mal may be just Galeno now. Omos watched the match from the stage.
7) Brutus Creed, Julius Creed b Aerostar, El Fiscal
## Earlier, to end the live show, the two Grande Americanos signed their mask match contract that required no physicality between them. Original Grande Americano claimed Andrea slapping him on the last taping made for an unsafe workplace and would only sign if AAA fired her. Kaiser Grande objected but Andrea told him to accept it and to win the mask, before being escorted out. After the signing, the Creeds attacked Kaiser Americano from behind, Los Americanos made the save. Creeds continued to beat up Aerostar after defeating him, and laid out Fiscal. Los Americanos tried to make the save, but Original Grande Americano took them out and tried to unmask Bravo. Kaiser Americano tried to make the save but was not allowed to touch Original and so couldn't get involved. Rayo finally made the save.
